<!---->
          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkımızda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              FONET Bilgi Teknolojileri is the leading medical informatics company of Turkey. FONET aims at regional leadership in the domain of digital medical applications. FONET’s global development approach is focused on leveraging the national experience we have acquired in strategically important markets worldwide. FONET provides all the hardware, software and infrastructure to the medical organizations in need of an automated integrated information management system.
 
To this end, system support units, technical support units and design units make sure to reflect the day to day conditions into the applications. Based on this work principle, the programs create a growing synergy between medical sector services and the services patient receives from the organization. Besides, based on highest level business partnerships with foreign sectoral leaders beta test programs are given utmost importance and all the novelties are presented to the customers as a first priority.
 
In "Technology Fast 500 EMEA 2011" survey carried out by Deloitte, FONET ranked in "Fast 50" category endorsing FONET's success as one of the fastest growing technology companies in the last five years based on year 2009 and year 2011 results. Having carried it's national success into the international arena, FONET is honoured to be first companys on initial 28 Turkish companies in Fast500 list covering Europe, Middle East and Africa regions.
          </p>
